As soon as Vivekananda started with \" Sisters and brothers of America\" the whole jam packed hall rose to their feet and gave him a standing ovation of more than 3 minutes --of inexplicable rapture.</em><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://1.gvt0.com/vi/N8MRaedvfUU/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/N8MRaedvfUU&fs=1&source=uds\" />\n<param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" />\n<embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/N8MRaedvfUU&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Two decades ago, while in the Pacific ocean, my Chief Officer told me a story when I went up to bullshit with him in his evening watch. </span></em><br />\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">He said that his family runs a restaurant on the Mumbai Pune highway. The Paav Vadas are so tasty, that even top&nbsp;film stars make sure they stop their cars and have it. </span></em><br />\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Then one day, the cook who had been serving their family for decades, suddenly decided to start his own&nbsp;restaurant&nbsp;nearby. And naturally, there was a switch of customer loyalty and &nbsp;exodus, to the other restaurant-- as all knew he was the guy who made the stuff. </span></em><br />\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Pretty soon, everybody came back , like prodigal son--total re-polarisation.&nbsp; And my Chief Offiecrs family was unable to figure out why the same cook could NOT make the same tasty fare again. </span></em><br />\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">The reason was given to them by their family pundit. In the middle of the restaurant yard , they had a huge shady Banyan tree. It was the&nbsp;energy vibes generated by the banyan tree which make the Paav so soft n fluffy ( burger buns basically ) and the Vada ( spicy&nbsp;potato bonda ) so tasty.</span></em><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Max Mueller who worked for drug running Rothschild owned British East India Company, was instructed by Thomas Babington Macaulay to belittle the great Hindu religion .&nbsp; It was all about Christianity and&nbsp;Judaism needing to shine, at the expense of Hinduism. How petty they could get is what follows.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-fL7k7jqtQCk/Tl0kn8Ta3BI/AAAAAAAAFzE/Y2D2o8-ejv0/s1600/imagesCANCMMBK.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-fL7k7jqtQCk/Tl0kn8Ta3BI/AAAAAAAAFzE/Y2D2o8-ejv0/s1600/imagesCANCMMBK.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-fEfbd_o6lK0/Tl0kl7vBuCI/AAAAAAAAFzA/nL0vYZPksOg/s1600/cnm.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-fEfbd_o6lK0/Tl0kl7vBuCI/AAAAAAAAFzA/nL0vYZPksOg/s1600/cnm.png\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It is written in the Rig Veda written in Sanskrit in 5000 BC, that the&nbsp;Vat Vriksha ( belittled by&nbsp;Vatican as the&nbsp;banyan tree , under which Banias held their shopkeeping business ) has a spiritual role in human life and must be revered. It was always a wonder as to how ageless a banyan tree can be. The tree which Alexander the great wrote in his records , as providing shelter to 8000 of his soldiers is still living. </span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-w_tDuUwfB40/Tl0pd6EP_FI/AAAAAAAAF0Y/PvUkBTS0F58/s1600/untitledvbn.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-w_tDuUwfB40/Tl0pd6EP_FI/AAAAAAAAF0Y/PvUkBTS0F58/s400/untitledvbn.png\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n&nbsp;&nbsp; <br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The tree symbolises eternal life, due to its unending expansion. It is also called the Kalpaka Vriksha or the wish full filling tree, in the Atharva Veda. In the Bhagawat Gita Lord Krishna praises the tree as immortal.Sanatana Dharma ( Hinduism ) is known as a giant banyan tree, under whose shade a thousand faiths bloom. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-qjil8UtrJvI/Tl0qQ7ZzUvI/AAAAAAAAF0c/Do1ZLCd21a0/s1600/imagesCAIN3M2T.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"254\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-qjil8UtrJvI/Tl0qQ7ZzUvI/AAAAAAAAF0c/Do1ZLCd21a0/s400/imagesCAIN3M2T.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">For this is a tree that does NOT grow out of the soil. It grows out of its own branches. The seed alights on the branch, germinates from there and produces handing roots that invade the soils to grow into a new tree. After a couple of centuries the host tree does NOT exist any more, like how the human race changes form.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In Bhagawat Gita Sri Krishna tells Prince Arjuna before the great war. \" Of all the trees I am the Banyan tree\". This is where the creation and destruction of the Cosmos comes. This concept of Singularity ( which even Einstein did NOT understand ) or the Bindu of the Sri Yantra sacred geometry, &nbsp;I will explain later in this same post.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ZAzKDyBIPk4/Tl0qabFkNtI/AAAAAAAAF0g/Xa-TAM4-kU4/s1600/untitledrg.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"298\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ZAzKDyBIPk4/Tl0qabFkNtI/AAAAAAAAF0g/Xa-TAM4-kU4/s400/untitledrg.png\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp; </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">So in 1858 German Jew Max Mueller, put the age of the Great banyan tree of Acharya Jagdish Chandra Bose Botanical garden , Howrah, near Calcutta to 60 years. So today if you see Rothschild promoted&nbsp;free encyclopedia &nbsp;Wikipedia on Internet, its says that this tree is just 200 years old. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-cJDyV-ruyPk/Tl2kwEeJBoI/AAAAAAAAF0o/ZfegU06uTR4/s1600/untitled.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"422\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-cJDyV-ruyPk/Tl2kwEeJBoI/AAAAAAAAF0o/ZfegU06uTR4/s640/untitled.png\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When Max Mueller saw this timeless milleniums old tree, it covered 4.8 acres of land or nearly 15000 square metres, with about 3000 aerial roots invading the soil as fresh trees--but all interlinked as one giant tree..as a great tangle of branches , roots and trunks. In those days this single tree looked like a great forest having a circumference of 1.2 kilometers. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-nJ4BW-Qxi28/Tl0mEp-a-GI/AAAAAAAAFzc/bYkBJG8sV4E/s1600/imagesCAH9GAJ5.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">How petty can human nature get -- how low can a human being be reduced to?</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-a8-wNWmLTHo/Tl0mUMv122I/AAAAAAAAFzg/EDSKKj8tKWs/s1600/imagesCAMXH0VZ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Rightly after Independence the Indian Govt has chosen Banyan tree as our national tree, for here is a&nbsp;&nbsp;a tree that regenerates unlike other trees, and is immortal unless sabotaged.. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-yBv59P9BWI8/Tl2k4DZHUxI/AAAAAAAAF0s/au1G-671Ke4/s1600/imagesCAO9ZF65.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"265\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-yBv59P9BWI8/Tl2k4DZHUxI/AAAAAAAAF0s/au1G-671Ke4/s400/imagesCAO9ZF65.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In every traditional Hindu temple there is a Banyan tree or a Peepal tree on the East side. Peepal is also called Bodhi tree, under which Gautama Buddha got enlightened 3900 years ago.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The Banyan tree is the male equivalent and Peepal is the female counterpart. The Peepal leaf is tender heart shaped which flaps with a gentle breeze and has a tapering long tail. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-23jt36q_OM0/Tl0mgUiS06I/AAAAAAAAFzk/5yNOZSa33X8/s1600/BANYAN.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-23jt36q_OM0/Tl0mgUiS06I/AAAAAAAAFzk/5yNOZSa33X8/s400/BANYAN.png\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The Banyan leaf is elliptical , shiny , stiff and&nbsp;leathery .The Peepal has a single truck while the larger and taller Banyan tree has several trunks. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-pbX8aqdtBrc/Tl0mxW7aMaI/AAAAAAAAFzo/zd6U6BFOGvQ/s1600/220px-Banyan_botanical_c1800-1830.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-pbX8aqdtBrc/Tl0mxW7aMaI/AAAAAAAAFzo/zd6U6BFOGvQ/s320/220px-Banyan_botanical_c1800-1830.jpg\" width=\"211\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The leaves contain water and even if you light a bonfire underneath , nothing happens to the leaves, as is seen at Sabarimala where thousands of coconuts are burnt with ghee in the havanam . The intelligence of the tree lies in teh water content of the leaves. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Every single village in India has a Banyan tree who stood as a mute spiritual witness to deeds conducted under it. Every village held court, without written records under it, the tree being the sole witness. Under this tree people do NOT tell lies, lest the spirits in the tree get offended. Provoking the spirits within the tree brings misfortune and ill health. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">So the mighty Banyan tree is the tree of knowledge and the tree of life, as it was the focus of the Panchayat community and the village council. Of course it provided as good&nbsp;&nbsp;shade and friendly vibes to hundreds of people who sat under it.. Instant justice was provided under the canopy of this majestic sacred tree of wisdom. People behaved themselves under a Banyan tree, where the village deity is installed. It was rather an outdoor temple, with the main truck having a platform built around it. .&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-xz575LP2ljA/Tl0nKAOn0jI/AAAAAAAAFzs/GI4sqS0z0YU/s1600/imagesCAZTZMH4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-xz575LP2ljA/Tl0nKAOn0jI/AAAAAAAAFzs/GI4sqS0z0YU/s400/imagesCAZTZMH4.jpg\" width=\"265\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It is about culture--people without culture will never understand this. In India when we are respectful to our parents , it is a part of our culture, and is programmed into our DNA. If you see America TV soaps, all for the sake of canned laughter, just see how a daughter insults her father of a son insults his mother, on wife insults the husband in front of her children. Thank god we do not have such bullshit uncultured serials in India even today. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-XEqI-j_DbSA/Tl0pJ1OoAhI/AAAAAAAAF0U/3y07aW0D2PQ/s1600/ta-prohm-banyan.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"480\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-XEqI-j_DbSA/Tl0pJ1OoAhI/AAAAAAAAF0U/3y07aW0D2PQ/s640/ta-prohm-banyan.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp; </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In ancient days the stutterers and the stammer party used to lick honey out of a Peepal leaf to get magic cures. Women keep vrat , walk clockwise around the tree 7 times , and tie sacred thread around the tree, to be removed when the vow is full filled.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Vsd3zq0RMwY/Tl0lt3Mu4qI/AAAAAAAAFzU/y4oOnu_PdJU/s1600/imagesCAIXXBQ0.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Vsd3zq0RMwY/Tl0lt3Mu4qI/AAAAAAAAFzU/y4oOnu_PdJU/s400/imagesCAIXXBQ0.jpg\" width=\"298\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Peepal leaf art has taken off in a bid way. You can soak a leaf in water and separate the pulp from the veins. The image of Lord Krishna as a young baby floating on a leaf down the river, sucking on the big toe is of particular religious significance. If you keep this image on a black background, the image comes alive. Remove the background and the image fades like magic.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-howwdEcFYQ0/Tl0l3D5t2sI/AAAAAAAAFzY/jFRyNrZ2bOw/s1600/imagesCA7Q9G33.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-howwdEcFYQ0/Tl0l3D5t2sI/AAAAAAAAFzY/jFRyNrZ2bOw/s400/imagesCA7Q9G33.jpg\" width=\"253\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">When you have a big bang which created the cosmos, you need to have a black hole singularity too.</span> This is commonsense which Albert Einstein and party ignored despite being very proficient with Indian Vedas. </span><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The Bindu of&nbsp;the Sri yantra represents singularity. The cosmos expands and contracts at regular cycles as explained by Sri Krishna in the Bhagawat Gita--just like inhalation and exhalation.</span><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><em>As per the Vedas the sole witness to the cosmic deluge is Maharishi Markandeya.</em> </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-q-nEUIt7I6M/Tl0o7HSt6mI/AAAAAAAAF0Q/RP8NcddQ8TA/s1600/krishna-on-leaf2s.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-q-nEUIt7I6M/Tl0o7HSt6mI/AAAAAAAAF0Q/RP8NcddQ8TA/s400/krishna-on-leaf2s.jpg\" width=\"386\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><em>&nbsp; </em></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><em>  </em></span><br />\n<div style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><em><span style=\"color: #cc0000;\"><span style=\"color: black;\">It was stated by the Lord in the Vedas: \u201cOh, Human! This village of yours is balanced on the banyan leaf and your lifespan is just a like a drop of water running down that leaf, which may fall any minute.\u201d</span> </span></em></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><em><span style=\"color: #cc0000;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><br /></span></span></em></span></div>\n<div style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><em>  </em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><em>Suddenly, amongst all the confusion, Markandeya noticed a banyan leaf floating on the ocean, tossed by the waves. On this unlikely raft lay a beautiful and adorable child, suckling his right toe, unperturbed by the calamity that had befallen the world. It was Krishna as Balaji, the newborn cosmic child.  </em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><em>The infant's heavenly smile negated the brutality of the pralaya (cosmic deluge). His compassionate glance reassured Markandeya that life would go on, convincing him that the world never ends, but only changes.</em></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><em>When Markandeya went close to this baby, he was sucked in with the air, when the baby took a breath. </em></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Inside, he saw hundreds of thousand of universes and all that had been consumed by the deluge - the skies, the seas, the earth, gods, demons, humans, animals and plants. </span></em></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><em>So much so, that he even had a glimpse of his own Ashram on the banks of the Subhadra River. He saw himself sitting in meditation. Markandeya thus realized that the child was none other than the cosmic god (Narayana) who had withdrawn the world into himself.</em> </span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IH8KhhqS3nQ/Tl0lXkfE84I/AAAAAAAAFzM/XXWaTl1yFCE/s1600/untitledYH.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IH8KhhqS3nQ/Tl0lXkfE84I/AAAAAAAAFzM/XXWaTl1yFCE/s400/untitledYH.png\" width=\"298\" /></a></span></div>\n</div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\">\n</span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"r\" style=\"margin: 1em 0in;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"mso-ansi-language: EN-GB; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial;\"><em>In that vast sea he again saw the banyan tree growing on the tiny island and the infant boy lying within the leaf. The child ( Vishnu ) glanced at him from the corner of His eyes with a smile imbued with the nectar of love, and Markandeya took Him into his heart through his eyes. Greatly agitated, the sage ran to embrace the transcendental Personality of Godhead.</em></span></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; Ajit Vadakayil</a></cite><span class=\"icon user blog-author\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;data:image/png; background-repeat: no-repeat; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px -4px 6px; width: 18px;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2011/08/banyan-tree-and-singularity-capt-ajit.html?showComment=1452346762600#c2039925041832993843\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">January 9, 2016 at 7:09 PM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nhi sd,<br /><br />sri-bhagavan uvaca--<br /><br />urdhva-mulam adhah-sakham<br />ashvattham prahur avyayam<br />chandamsi yasya parnani<br />yas tam veda sa veda-vit<br /><br />Translation: The Blessed Lord said, \u201cThere is a banyan tree which has its roots upward and its branches down and whose leaves are the Vedic hymns. One who knows this tree is the knower of the Vedas.\u201d<br /><br />The tree of cosmic existence has no beginning and no end, n\u0101nto na c\u0101dih, in space or in time; for it is eternal and imperishable, avyaya. The hymns of the Veda are compared to its leaves and the man who knows this tree of the cosmos is the Veda-knower.<br /><br />Lord Krishna tells Arjuna in the Kuruskhetra field , just before the war 6000 years ago-<br /><br />\" This world is a Banyan tree whose roots are above and branches below, and whose attractive leaves are promises of enjoyment. He who knows this tree well knows the methods of gaining such enjoyment. Watered by the three qualities of nature, its branches expand in all directions, upwards and downwards, finally producing buds of enjoyable sense objects. From these branches, roots also fall downwards and find nourishment in the selfish deeds of the mortal world\"<br /><br />You must search out what is beyond it; some place from which no one ever strays. There, finally, seek for that Original Person \u2013 the ancient one from whom the true tree grows \u2013 and give yourself to him.<br /><br />The upside-down tree is the banyan tree, representing the material world, which is a perverted reflection of the spiritual world. The demigods are on the top branches, the human beings are on the middle branches, and the animals are on the lower branches. A man disentangles himself from the tree by cutting it with the WEAPON OF DETACHMENT.<br /><br />The entanglement of this material world is compared here to a banyan tree. For one who is engaged in fruitive activities, there is no end to the banyan tree. He wanders from one branch to another, to another, to another. The tree of this material world has no end, and for one who is attached to this tree, there is no possibility of liberation. The Vedic hymns, meant for elevating oneself, are called the leaves of this tree. This tree's roots grow upward because they begin from where Brahma is located, the topmost planet of this universe. If one can understand this indestructible tree of MAYA (illusion) , then one can get out of it.<br /><br />The banyan tree can be found beside a reservoir of temple pond water. We can see that the trees on the bank reflect upon the water with their branches down and roots up. The tree of this material world is only a reflection of the real tree of the spiritual world. This reflection of the spiritual world is situated on desire, just as a tree's reflection is on water. Desire is the cause of things being situated in this reflected material light. One who wants to get out of this material existence must know this tree thoroughly through study of the Vedas . Then he can cut off his relationship with it.<br /><br />A reflection is temporary, for it is sometimes seen and sometimes not seen. But the origin from whence the reflection is reflected is eternal. The material reflection of the real tree has to be cut off.<br /><br />When it is said that a person knows the Vedas, it is assumed that he knows how to cut off attachment to this material world. If one knows that process, he actually knows the Vedas.<br /><br />One who is attracted by the ritualistic formulas of the Vedas is attracted by the beautiful green leaves of the tree. He does not exactly know the true purpose of the Vedas.<br /><br />The purpose of the Vedas, as disclosed by the Personality of Godhead Himself, is to CUT DOWN THE REFLECTED TREE and attain the real tree of the spiritual world.<br /><br />TO UNDERSTAND THIS PROFOUND TRUTH, EVERY TEMPLE HAS A WATER BODY WITH A BANYAN TREE REFLECTED IN THE WATER.<br /><br />CONTINUED TO 2-</div>\n<span class=\"comment-actions secondary-text\"><span class=\"item-control blog-admin blog-admin pid-1783552029\" style=\"display: inline;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-replies\" style=\"margin-left: 36px; margin-top: 1em;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-replybox-single\" id=\"c2039925041832993843-ce\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; margin-top: 5px;\">\n</div>\n</li>\n<li class=\"comment\" id=\"c4425918688286105749\" style=\"border-bottom: 0px; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0.25em 0px 0px;\"><div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"float: left; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">Capt. After one enjoys the results of virtuous activities in the upper planetary systems ( one of the lower 6 dimensions ) , he comes down to this earth to lighten his KARMIC BAGGAGE , in the hope of attaining the topmost 7th dimension for MOKSHA.<br /><br />\"The real form of this tree cannot be perceived in this world. No one can understand where it ends, where it begins, or where its foundation is. But with determination one must cut down this tree with the weapon of detachment. So doing, one must seek that place from which, having once gone, one never returns, and there surrender to that Supreme Personality of Godhead from whom everything has began and in whom everything is abiding since time immemorial.<br /><br />aham sarvasya prabhavah, \"I am the origin of everything.\"<br /><br />To get out of the entanglement of this strong banyan tree of material life, one must surrender to Krishna. <br />\n<br />\nIt is about accepting some rigid self discipline and sticking to it. <br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">People when they want to even TURN OVER A NEW LEAF , do a vrat as a ritual. It is a thousand times more stronger than a bullshit new year resolution.</span><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-VaxB4l7BbQE/TlvjYlVm7eI/AAAAAAAAFys/7kpZjoQ1x5M/s1600/imagesCA01AUD8.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-VaxB4l7BbQE/TlvjYlVm7eI/AAAAAAAAFys/7kpZjoQ1x5M/s1600/imagesCA01AUD8.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThis is always a goal in mind. It is about harnessing&nbsp;your meandering mind , which aids self focus to awaken your dormant powers within. <br />\n<br />\nVrat has been given pride of place in Sanatana Dharma or Hinduism. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-LHy2UAoECfY/TlvjeXWi6mI/AAAAAAAAFyw/sZVvkzZyYec/s1600/imagesCAT92BCM.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-LHy2UAoECfY/TlvjeXWi6mI/AAAAAAAAFyw/sZVvkzZyYec/s1600/imagesCAT92BCM.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nYou don't harm anybody by doing your Vrat. The practical aspect is linked a lot to regulation of diet or even abstaining from sex , rather some type of austerity.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">It has a spiritual tinge&nbsp;and hence it sends a message to an onlooker about how resolute you are in achieving your goal,&nbsp; that you are firm as a rock and unwilling to surrender to destiny--that you plan to forge the hinges of your destiny on your own terms.</span> <br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">Non-violence, love, truth , unselfishness, sacrifice, grace, honesty form the warp and weft of this vrat fabric.&nbsp; Optimism , courage , perseverance , contemplation and fortitude form the fibre.</span><br />\n<br />\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-TMw636tEaYo/Tlveu3isGeI/AAAAAAAAFyQ/HGHvnmC7ovo/s1600/imagesCA32KW0M.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-TMw636tEaYo/Tlveu3isGeI/AAAAAAAAFyQ/HGHvnmC7ovo/s1600/imagesCA32KW0M.jpg\" /></a><br />\n<br />\nLet me talk about a Sabarimala pilgrimage Vratam.<br />\n<br />\nLet is be on record that Sabarimala attracted 48 million pilgrims on the season which ended in Jan 14th sunset, at Makara Vilakku (Sankranti) &nbsp;day.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-wILXypwCYnU/Tlve3V6jzMI/AAAAAAAAFyU/nR8u1U9EyBI/s1600/acv.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-wILXypwCYnU/Tlve3V6jzMI/AAAAAAAAFyU/nR8u1U9EyBI/s1600/acv.png\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\nOn Makara Vilakku day itself 1.4 million pilgrims thronged at this small hillock. The temple collected 1.3 billion US dollars, in a season of 2 months<br />\n<br />\nMecca Kaaba in comparison attracts just 1.8 million pilgrims annually.&nbsp; The great Kumbh Mela attracts just 45 million pilgrims. This makes Sabarimala the largest pilgrim centre on this planet.<br />\n<br />\nSabarimala temple is a Hindu pilgrimage centre&nbsp;on the Western Ghats mountain range of Kerala. A divine light ( a Vedic camphor homam ) is lit as an unbroken tradition since the past 6000 years.<br />\n<br />\n<em>The Vatican has fudged records to make Lord Ayyapan a recent phenomenon.&nbsp; There is a mosque on the forest trek path. It is a very ancient temple converted into a mosque. The Vatican and the Jews ( Rothschild ) , to show that their religions are older have cooked up imaginary conversations between a Muslim and Lord Ayyappa.&nbsp; Islam&nbsp; is a recent religion like Christianity, and Judaism , while Hinduism or Sanatana Dharma is 11000 years old.</em><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-FyTXe2Qk68A/Tlvfa6dCqDI/AAAAAAAAFyk/ol0t3qRMz3Y/s1600/cvb.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-FyTXe2Qk68A/Tlvfa6dCqDI/AAAAAAAAFyk/ol0t3qRMz3Y/s1600/cvb.png\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe pilgrims have to observe a 41 day VRAT or penance , before they go to the temple . There are no cheaters. Nobody monitors, as it is about your own mind cleansing.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-m8OSZrjufWc/TlvfoaHRKYI/AAAAAAAAFyo/TKFkmmb1pOQ/s1600/untitled.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-m8OSZrjufWc/TlvfoaHRKYI/AAAAAAAAFyo/TKFkmmb1pOQ/s1600/untitled.png\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nFor 41 days the pilgrims abstain from sex, alcohol, cigarettes, non-vegetarian food, foul language and&nbsp; lack of discipline.<br />\n<br />\nThey have to wear&nbsp;black cotton clothes, be barefooted ( in preparation for a steep forest mountain trail trek ) &nbsp;and cannot shave or cut their hair, to remind them of their vrat and their determination&nbsp; keep away from worldly objects of pleasure, and NOT to hurt the feelings of others.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-pnyR7rO6ht4/TlvfKdfaCuI/AAAAAAAAFyc/bRoO5te55SY/s1600/imagesCA5B3HRT.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-pnyR7rO6ht4/TlvfKdfaCuI/AAAAAAAAFyc/bRoO5te55SY/s1600/imagesCA5B3HRT.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThey have to bathe twice a day and visit the local temple to offer prayers. They sleep for 41 days on the floor without pillows. Sabarimala pilgrimage is a great leveller. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-8-Q8YrOxClw/TlvfDIHrLMI/AAAAAAAAFyY/vxQwFGqTntI/s1600/wer.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-8-Q8YrOxClw/TlvfDIHrLMI/AAAAAAAAFyY/vxQwFGqTntI/s1600/wer.png\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nOn the first day the pilgrim will be initiated by a Guru Swami, who has undertaken 18 successive years of Sabarimala pilgrimage. He has to present himself after a bath, clean shaven with nails trimmed. A sanctified Mala or garland of Rudrakha beads is put on the neck, while chanting the mantra, \"Swamiye &nbsp;Sharanamayyappa\" . Women between 9 and 50 cannot be pilgrims.<br />\n<br />\nAt the moment of Makaravikkaku millions of throats look at a single light and chant an electriying and hair rasing \"Swamiye  Sharanamayyappa\". This sends out a soliton field over the planet.&nbsp; Millions of coconuts are broken. It was shipped across in Rosewood containers, available only in Kerala-- to prevent oxidation.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-YNdhKfUk05k/TlqEkg0ScZI/AAAAAAAAFxs/75-OT3ZS2KE/s1600/imagesCAHB9CP7.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-YNdhKfUk05k/TlqEkg0ScZI/AAAAAAAAFxs/75-OT3ZS2KE/s1600/imagesCAHB9CP7.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThis honey was superior AAA grade and in addition was <span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">ENHANCED BY SCALAR ENERGY</span> EMANATING FROM THE 12 STRAND DNA OF MAHARSHIS. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-4nvZy112ywA/TlqErwst_eI/AAAAAAAAFxw/9e2H3Orxye0/s1600/imagesCAFWW6P4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-4nvZy112ywA/TlqErwst_eI/AAAAAAAAFxw/9e2H3Orxye0/s1600/imagesCAFWW6P4.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe honey gets deteriorated by high temperatures in Egypt otherwise. It also prevents battle scars.<br />\n<br />\nEven today Kerala hardly does artificial bee hive keeping. The honey in hives exist on trees in the western ghat forests in great abundance. This natural honey has a rich distinctive aroma.&nbsp; This scent is the&nbsp;same aromatic volatile oils in the fresh wild tropical flowers&nbsp;. <br />\n<br />\nThis natural nectar taken in by the bees has very high sugar concentration. Ordinarily to obtain 450 grams ( a small bottle ) of pure honey, 16000 bees must visit 9.5 million flowers--around 7200 work hours. <br />\n<br />\nThe 3 different sugars are dextrose (34% ) , sucrose ( 2%) and fructose (40% ) water ( 17% ) and 7 % of minerals, vitamins, elements, acids, hormones and proteins. <br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: x-large;\">This 7% is what the quality of honey is all about.</span> <br />\n<br />\nIf the nectar is taken from a good rich nectar source the honey works quantum magic&nbsp;on the&nbsp; human body .<br />\n<br />\nIn the hive the bees use their honey stomachs to ingest and REGURGITATE several times till it is digested, and the end product reached a desired quality. Only then it is stored in honeycomb cells.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nAfter the final regurgitation the honey cell is left unsealed, for it is still high in water content and natural yeasts, which can cause fermentation.. The bees now use their wings as fans to evaporate the water. This raises the sugar concentration too.<br />\n<br />\nNowadays useless artificial honey from bees force fed with artificial sugar and molasses in bee hives,&nbsp;has bacteria in it. I was a young strapping Chief Mate of the SCI ship Vishwa Ajay. It was a fantastic multipurpose ship, made in Warnemunde. It could do 25 knots, had huge jumbo derricks, was fully automated , and could make profit on a voyage by just carrying refrigerated cargo, or vegetable oils in deep tanks.<br />\n<br />\nBut it had a serious problem. All six sister A class ships had stability problems.&nbsp; By the time I joined Vishwa Ajay, 3 of the sister ships had angle off loll and became unstable with huge list. In fact just as I joined Vishwa Amitabh has a angle of loll in-- hold your breath--Bombay lock gates. The first two ships one of them was Vishwa Aditya had angle of loll while taking to the blocks at dry docks.<br />\n<br />\nWe were due for dry docks and the ship was discharging at Hamburg, just before dry docking at HDW dry dock. I was given instructions NOT to discharge hold no 1 , which contained coffee beans in bags. This was to bring the trim down from 20 feet to a reasonable 4 feet.<br />\n<br />\nAs soon as the Tech Suptd came from SCI Bombay, I told him to arrange for a meeting with the drydock bosses. I had to bypass the Captain who had come up from the ranks and had zilch understanding of stability ( no names ) --his nick name was <a href=\"mailto:fuck-knows-step*@#$&amp;se\"><span style=\"color: black;\">fuck-knows-step*#$&amp;se</span></a>--I can see many of you smiling wryly already.<br />\n<br />\nThe German yard&nbsp;bosses came , quite qualified and intelligent&nbsp;men. I told them \" I want to avoid dry docking in a graving dock with coffee beans in No 1 hold, as the quality will get deteriorated with paint spray , lack of ventilation etc. Is it possible for the ship to dry-dock at that HDW floating dry dock.\"<br />\n<br />\nI took them to the porthole and pointed it out. \"The idea is to reduce the virtual loss of GM due to upthrust while taking the aft most block, at nearly 16 feet of trim\".<br />\n<br />\nThey did NOT understand , so I had to go to the blackboard and explain with formulas and diagrams. Where the dry dock would be trimmed , so that the difference between the trims of dock blocks and the ship's keel would be just 4 feet. <br />\n<br />\nSuddenly the hull side young boss said \" Yes, Chief , I have studied ship stability , I know what you mean. I will give you the answer tomorrow PM !.&nbsp; Meanwhile congratulations-- You may be knowing that such an attempt will be the&nbsp;FIRST on this planet\"<br />\n<br />\nLater at night, we had gone out to Reeperbahn ( St Pauli ) and while having a couple beers , my junior officer said \" Saab, I have heard of you from your&nbsp;batch mates. Your nick-name as a cadet was Mr India , right?.&nbsp; Half of it was because of your muscles and the other half for always saying again and again that India would be world's No 1 super-power country by 2020, and that Brazil would be No 2.&nbsp; Saab,<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"> today you made me proud of being an Indian</span> .&nbsp; The&nbsp;highly qualified Germans were in awe of you.&nbsp;\"<br />\n<br />\nI laughed it off&nbsp; \" Only if India can root out corruption-- and Brazilians think sex , booze and music ain't everything!\" <br />\n<span style=\"color: black;\">.</span><br />\nOf course, &nbsp;we did the docking after 3 days on a floating HDW Hamburg dry dock, with entire cargo discharged --and the dry dock trimmed . <br />\n<br />\nWhen the ship sat on the blocks , I as the Chief Officer sat in the control room of the shore dry dock. &nbsp;Any problems, with dock trimming / ballasting and &nbsp;I would abort, before the floating dry dock and the ship capsized in the water-- a terrible disaster to imagine .<br />\n<br />\nTo calculate virtual loss of GM :-<br />\n<br />\n<em>P= t X MCTC/ LCF ( t is trim in cms )</em><br />\n<em>virtual loss of GM= PX KM/W ( where W is displacement in tonnes )</em><br />\n<br />\nNot many people realise that KM reduces with trim. This is why the 3 A class ships had angle of loll.<br />\n<br />\nI had made sure of the fluid GM of W =Vishwa Ajay by shifting the heavy jumbo boom suddenly, and measuring the period of roll with a stop watch --and averaged it over 5 attempts.<br />\n<br />\n<em>Square root of GM&nbsp; ( feet ) = 0.44 X&nbsp; (breadth in feet / Time period of roll in seconds) .</em><br />\n<br />\nMany years&nbsp;later Vishwa Anuraag and Vishwa Apurva would sink at sea.<br />\n<br />\nAnother 9 years before we get to 2020.&nbsp; Corrupt Indians have stashed away 3 TRILLION US dollars of slush money in foreign banks and lockers ( gold/ diamonds ) &nbsp;-- Swiss banks have 1.8 trillion of this.money in currency alone\"<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-mGL0Ng_JbhA/Tlkg3SDrR4I/AAAAAAAAFw8/4YsXg9t3_ao/s1600/imagesCA2L3RFA.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-mGL0Ng_JbhA/Tlkg3SDrR4I/AAAAAAAAFw8/4YsXg9t3_ao/s1600/imagesCA2L3RFA.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nAnna Hazare had given hope to 1.2 billion Indians who are sick and tired of rampant, brazen corruption. Where the nation's prime minister Manmohan Singh declares that his hands are tied due to compulsions of coalition politics, and that he does NOT have a magic wand . Ajit Vadakayil December 6, 2016 at 1:49 PM<br />IMPORTANT....... IMPORTANT...... IMPORTANT.......... THE WARSHIP INS BETWA , CAPSIZED WHILE UNDOCKING FROM DRYDOCK , DUE TO STABILITY CALCULATIONS NOT BEING DONE PROPERLY ..................... I AM A SHIP CAPTAIN WITH 30 YEARS EXPERIENCE ............. VIRTUAL LOSS OF GM DUE TO UPTHRUST .................... To calculate virtual loss of GM :-............. P= t X MCTC/ LCF ( t is trim in cms )....... virtual loss of GM= PX KM/W ( where W is displacement in tonnes ).............&nbsp;<span style=\"color: blue;\">Not many people realise that KM reduces with increase of trim................this is the reason why docking/ undocking trim by stern must be as small as possible\u2026\u2026\u2026.. while undocking the most critical and dangerous period is when the ship is afloat with only the aftermost part of keel resting on the aftermost block</span>\u2026\u2026\u2026\u2026 \u2026\u2026\u2026\u2026..FIRST STEP TO SALVAGE THE PATHETIC INDIAN NAVY IS TO CHANGE THE COLOUR OF THEIR UNIFORM FROM WHITE TO KHAKHI............. ALL RESPONSIBLE PEOPLE INCLUDING THE CAPTAIN MUST BE SACKED......... THIS IS SHEER INCOMPETENCE...........&nbsp;<span style=\"color: purple;\">The interval of time between the stern post landing on the blocks and the ship taking the blocks overall is referred to as the critical period....... During this period part of the weight of the ship is being borne by the blocks, and this creates an upthrust at the stern which increases as the water level falls in the drydock. ......The upthrust causes a virtual loss in metacentric height and it is essential that positive effective metacentric height be maintained throughout the critical period, or the ship will heel over and perhaps slip off the blocks with disastrous results.&nbsp;</span>....capt ajit vadakayil ..<br /><span style=\"color: red;\"><br />http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2011/08/india-stands-tall-capt-ajit-vadakayil.html</span><br /><br />############################<br /><br />WE ASK NIRMALA SITARAMAN TO ADDRESS THE PROBLEM NOW .. , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-jY8bXZCnRhU/TlhXZtA4IWI/AAAAAAAAFwk/9SN2GiR6ejU/s1600/imagesCAZU6DUT.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-jY8bXZCnRhU/TlhXZtA4IWI/AAAAAAAAFwk/9SN2GiR6ejU/s1600/imagesCAZU6DUT.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Varahamihira's mathematical work included the discovery of the trigonometric formulas--</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">sin <i>x</i> = cos(p/2 - <i>x</i>), <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">sin2<i>x</i> + cos2<i>x</i> = 1, and <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">(1 - cos 2<i>x</i>)/2 = sin2<i>x</i>. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Varahamihira worked together on the sine tables with Aryabhata and calculated the binomial coefficients, known in the European civilization as Pascal's triangle.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-MX3hC_WHUEM/TlhWGt9m3BI/AAAAAAAAFwM/3ejJI9sT4T8/s1600/imagesCAEYXZVZ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-MX3hC_WHUEM/TlhWGt9m3BI/AAAAAAAAFwM/3ejJI9sT4T8/s1600/imagesCAEYXZVZ.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Among Varahamihira's contribution to physics is his statement that reflection is caused by the back-scattering of particles and refraction (the change of direction of a light ray as it moves from one medium into another) by the ability of the particles to penetrate inner spaces of the material, much like fluids that move through porous objects.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-mIlNb4mfTkQ/TlfypdGAF-I/AAAAAAAAFu8/hzJ2J8kHHZ8/s1600/imagesCAEYER1Y.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-mIlNb4mfTkQ/TlfypdGAF-I/AAAAAAAAFu8/hzJ2J8kHHZ8/s1600/imagesCAEYER1Y.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">The Kerala school of mathematics investigated rules for computing the number of ways in which <i>r</i> objects can be selected from <i>n</i> objects over the course of many hundreds of years. They gave rules to compute the binomial coefficients <i><sub>n</sub>C<sub>r</sub></i> which amount to <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><sub><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">n</span></sub></i><i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">C<sub>r</sub></span></i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"> = <i>n</i>(<i>n</i>-1)(<i>n</i>-2)...(<i>n</i>-<i>r</i>+1)/<i>r</i></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">However, Varahamihira attacked the problem of computing <i><sub>n</sub>C<sub>r</sub></i> in a rather different way. He wrote the numbers <i>n</i> in a column with <i>n</i> = 1 at the bottom. He then put the numbers <i>r</i> in rows with <i>r</i> = 1 at the left-hand side. Starting at the bottom left side of the array which corresponds to the values <i>n</i> = 1, <i>r</i> = 1, the values of <i><sub>n</sub>C<sub>r</sub></i> are found by summing two entries, namely the one directly below the (<i>n</i>, <i>r</i>) position and the one immediately to the left of it. This was later lifted by Pascal-- triangle for finding the binomial coefficients.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">He wrote treatises on <i>shakuna</i> ( augury ) as well as the <i>Brihaj-Jataka</i> (\u201cGreat Birth\u201d) and the <i>Laghu-Jataka</i> (\u201cShort Birth\u201d), two well-known works on the casting of horoscopes</span><br />\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-O6FqNYI5Y6U/TlfyhfIPXcI/AAAAAAAAFu4/_Oh2c0yEst8/s1600/9788120800984.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-O6FqNYI5Y6U/TlfyhfIPXcI/AAAAAAAAFu4/_Oh2c0yEst8/s1600/9788120800984.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Here is a popular story-- </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></em></div>\n<em><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span></em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; margin: 0in 0in 9pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Mihira Muni was accurate in his astrological predictions and predicted that the King's 18 year old son would be killed by a Varaha or a wild boar. He had also predicted the time as 5pm in the evening. Upon hearing these predictions from Mihira, the King gave orders to construct a special and secure palace for the royal prince.<o:p></o:p></span></em></span></div>\n<em><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span></em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; margin: 0in 0in 9pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">After the construction , as many as 10,000 troops were on high alert to meet any eventuality within and outside the palace area. Not even a rat was allowed to sneak in. Such was the security.<o:p></o:p></span></em></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-p0Fi_SsjIOE/TlhXl08nHAI/AAAAAAAAFwo/KdHtMu3h79k/s1600/untitled.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-p0Fi_SsjIOE/TlhXl08nHAI/AAAAAAAAFwo/KdHtMu3h79k/s1600/untitled.png\" /></span></a></div>\n<em><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span></em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background: white; margin: 0in 0in 9pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">On the fateful day, Mihira was told to rethink of his predictions. People started doubting Mihira\u2019s ability of foretelling. But he was firm in his words. Prince was seen happily playing with other children on the seventh floor of the palace where he used to be like a person under house arrest. But when the fateful time came, he went upstairs and to the open terrace. Meanwhile everyone thought Mihira would soon lose his recognition as astrologer. Mihira told the King that the prince had died and was lying in a pool of blood. <o:p></o:p></span></em></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8wwH7Ly3MHA/TlhXGN0WyOI/AAAAAAAAFwc/LvJNEALxULg/s1600/imagesCAY3QCQ4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8wwH7Ly3MHA/TlhXGN0WyOI/AAAAAAAAFwc/LvJNEALxULg/s1600/imagesCAY3QCQ4.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<em><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span></em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; margin: 0in 0in 9pt;\">\n<div style=\"background-color: white;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Everyone rushed to the terrace when the time was 6pm, only to see the prince lying in a pool of blood. No one knew why the boy went there to play. Prince was disfigured by the iron hooves of the artificial metal boar, the Royal Emblem attached to the flag staff. The King honored and gave him the title Varahamihira for his accuracy in astrology.</span></em></span></div>\n<div style=\"background-color: white;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"background-color: white; clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-TAMa61n1ztQ/TlhWNJS9ymI/AAAAAAAAFwQ/pDE7xJqz0Ec/s1600/imagesCAB3V7VS.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-TAMa61n1ztQ/TlhWNJS9ymI/AAAAAAAAFwQ/pDE7xJqz0Ec/s1600/imagesCAB3V7VS.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div style=\"background-color: white;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">Parameshawaran ( 1380\u20131460 AD ), was a Kerala mathematician&nbsp;, from whose work <span style=\"color: red;\">Sir Isaac Newton stole his entire Calculus</span>, without elementary understanding</span>.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; Ajit Vadakayil</a></cite><span class=\"icon user blog-author\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;data:image/png; background-repeat: no-repeat; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px -4px 6px; width: 18px;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2017/12/blockchain-bitcoin-big-brother-will.html?showComment=1513185259860#c4671100578196233665\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888;\">December 13, 2017 at 10:44 PM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_175MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nPhysicists in China and the US have built a 10-qubit superconducting quantum processor that could be scaled up to tackle problems not solvable by classical computers.<br />\n<br />\nQubits are the building blocks of quantum computing, capable of superposition \u2013 being in two states at the same time, rather than the computer bits of today, which are either a 1 or a 0 at any given moment.<br />\n<br />\nEntanglement is where quantum states can't be described independently, but only in relation to the others, making for a more solid system. The team used a measurement technique called quantum tomography to prove that they had indeed entangled their qubits<br />\n<br />\nThe phenomenon of entanglement in quantum physics, which has been observed in many experiments, implies that objects that are far removed in space (even across billions of miles) remain connected even though there is no mediating agency.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2011/01/quantum-entanglement-video-capt-ajit.html</span><br />\n<br />\nVedic philosophy tells us about the existence of another type of particle called the atma, the soul, the self, having different properties from those of ordinary particles.This is not unusual in physics, as is the case with antimatter particles.<br />\n<br />\nThe atma does not come into or out of existence, it is always present. It does not decay or degrade, it maintains its individuality always, it\u2019s infinitesimally small and it\u2019s not composed of more elementary particles. It\u2019s unchangeable, which along with the individuality property implies that it does not unite with other particles to create more complex structures, nor does it merge with others.<br />\n<br />\nThe atma does not interact directly with matter, but given that the atma is the source of consciousness and the life force in a living entity, any entity displaying them reveals the presence of an atma in it\u2014whether human, animal, plant, etc.<br />\n<br />\nVedanta wrote 7000 years ago-- The living entities are not made up of atmas; rather, they are these particles and are animating the material bodies that encase them. As soon as the atma leaves one body for another, the old body no longer exhibits consciousness or life symptoms, and begins to degrade.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2011/02/daltons-atomic-theory-sage-kashyapa-and.html</span><br />\n<br />\nMaharishi Kashyapa is also known as Kanada Muni. He called the atom Anu. He wrote that there are 108 such elements ...<br />\n<br />\nThe basic Vaisheshika concepts of matter, action, attribute, time and space are described. The 8500 year old Nyaya-Vaiseshika Sutra of Kanada Muni consists of 373 Sutras and is composed of 12 chapters.<br />\n<br />\nIt\u2019s main postulates are:--<br />\n<br />\nAll of the universe is composed of the 5 mahabhuttas and the 4 non physicals: that is Fluid, Atomic elements, fields/force, energy, ether and space, time, mind and soul.<br />\n<br />\nExcept ether, all of the physical elements are made of discreet and distinct paramanus or atoms<br />\n<br />\nSpace-time is a frame in which the physical universe exists<br />\n<br />\nThere are seven categories of experience, which are substance, quality, activity, generality, particularity, inherence, and nonexistence.<br />\n<br />\nEnergy and mass are equivalent.<br />\n<br />\nHere are some of the Sutras: ---<br />\n<br />\nForce is that which displaces, holds together or moves things apart.V.S 1.1.20<br />\nIn the absence of a force, a particle of matter experiences no change. V.S 1.1.6<br />\nThe forces to be considered are an external force, gravity, that with causes attraction of particles, that which causes repulsion of particles and the internal movements of them in matter.<br />\n<br />\nV.S 1.1.13 Action is opposed by an equivalent opposite reaction<br />\nV.S 5.1.1618 The diversities of the movement of an arrow are due to the consecutive changes in the components of the acting forces. The stored energy provides the propulsion to the arrow and this causes it move further to a high point. This component keeps reducing while that of gravity increases resulting in its fall.Once the work against gravity ceases then the body reaches an energyless state falling under gravity.<br />\nV.S 1.1.27 The force on a body is the resultant of gravity and the work done against it.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nCONTINUED TO 2-</div>\n</div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c5923840167230626705\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_173M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_173MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nCONTINUED FROM 1-<br />\n<br />\nV.S 5.1.13 In the absence of all other forces (saMyogabindings) gravity exists.<br />\nV.S 5.1.7 The \u201cguna\u201d of forces (direction) prevents a magnitude from being obtained<br />\nV.S.1.1.20a The nature of physical changes in matter is the terms of work being done on the basic particles that constitute matter.<br />\nV.S 2.1.14 The particular nature of air is suggested by the mixing of gases that occurs on their collision. Despite of being made of atoms and occupying space air fails show orderly movement so its form cannot be perceived<br />\nV.S 4.1.8 Solids occupy space and assume form due to conglomeration of the constituent particles.<br />\nV.S 4.1.6 The (fluid\u2019s) particles possess energy. This causes them to possess the property of fluidity. The heat bearing rays provide the particles with energy to form a gas and rise. The heated particles of air impact the vapor and with this energy it mixes with it. Freezing and melting of a liquid as being a result of heat being taken up or given up by its particles.<br />\nV.S 5.2.9 Some apparently solid substances like ghee, lac and wax are in reality liquids, as their particles are naturally \u201cheat-conjoined\u201d or disorganized as in water. Other true solid substances such as tin, lead, iron, silver and gold need their atoms to be supplied with external heat to disorder them before they become a fluid.<br />\nV.S 2.1.67 Any body\u2019s mass needs to be wholly explained in terms of its constituent particles.<br />\nV.S 1.1.89 A substance can only emerge from another substance and not on its own eventhough its properties change from one to another.<br />\nV.S 9.1.9 Any fundamental particular entity can be a constituent multiple substances.<br />\nV.S 1.1.22 Any substance comprising of two or more primary particle types requires a chemical reaction to generate the conjoining and break up of preexisting molecules.<br />\nV.S 1.1.23 The \u201cmolecules\u201d are stated as emerging from combinations between the fundamental entities.<br />\nV.S 1.1.25 Forces are necessary to bring about combination and break up of molecules.<br />\nV.S 1.1.28 The combinations of particles to produce molecules result in substances with states very different from those of the original particles.<br />\n<br />\nKanada Muni\u2019s laws:<br />\n<br />\nIn the production or increment of karma (i.e. motion), the root cause is force. In other words, there is incremental or decremental change in motion.<br />\nThis law is a law of the measure of force. According to this, so long mechanical force works, there is change in motion i.e. there is momentum. To find its value, it is calculated how much work it produces in a unit time.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nCONTINUED TO 3</div>\n<span class=\"comment-actions secondary-text\" id=\"bc_0_173MN\" kind=\"m\"><span class=\"item-control blog-admin pid-1783552029\" style=\"display: inline;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-replies\" id=\"bc_0_173BR\" style=\"margin-left: 36px; margin-top: 1em;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-replybox-single\" id=\"bc_0_173B_box\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; margin-top: 5px;\">\n</div>\n</li>\n<li class=\"comment\" id=\"bc_0_174B\" kind=\"b\" style=\"border-bottom: 0px; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0.25em 0px 0px;\"><div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"float: left; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c466643263114631994\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_174M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_174MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nCONTINUED FROM 2--<br />\n<br />\nMathematically, the rate of change in momentum i.e. the increment in work in unit time is proportional to the force in action. Also, this change is in the direction of the force. Suppose that the mass of an object is \u2018m\u2019 and in time interval \u2018t\u2019, the velocity of the object changes from \u2018u\u2019 to \u2018v\u2019 due to the force acting on it.<br />\n<br />\nThen, Initial momentum = m*u<br />\nFinal momentum = m*v<br />\nChange in momentum = m(v*u)<br />\nTherefore, the rate of change of momentum = m(v*u)/t<br />\nt = m*a (from Kanada\u2019s first law)<br />\n<br />\nFrom Kandas second law, force is proportional to the rate of change of momentum<br />\nOr, p = k*m*a (where k is a constant)<br />\nIf m=1 and a=1, then<br />\n1 = k*1*1 or k = 1<br />\nOr, p = m*a<br />\n<br />\nTherefore, unit force is the one that produces unit acceleration in an object of unit mass. The VS then goes to say that force is a result of work and is not a physical quantity which is superior to Newtons law that measures it as a physical quantity.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2011/01/isaac-newton-calculus-thief-capt-ajit.html</span><br />\n<br />\nThe sutras on energy:<br />\n<br />\nVaiseshika defines energy as being a radiant thing(i.e. energy is radiation) and energy is related totemperature and motion of a particle.<br />\n<br />\nVedic Indians understood the process of refraction and absorbtion of energy by \u201cmaterial obstructions\u201d and they understood heat, electricity and magnetism to be forms of energy. It is already understood by the elemental theory that light is also an energy and is composed of discreet units.<br />\n<br />\nThis was of course was not understood in modern times till Max Plank and Einstein in the 20th cetury devised quantum theory after the study of black body radiation and the photoelectric effect.<br />\n<br />\nCapt ajit vadakayil<br />\n..</div>\n</div>\n</li>\n</span></ol>\n<span id=\"bc_0_175b+seedBBVAD\" kind=\"d\">\n</span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; Use Emergency Manual Mode to shut down valves.&nbsp;&nbsp; All pump controls to be reset to off position, and all valves set to closed postion prior to resoration of power. &nbsp; Once power is regained, do NOT resume cargo UNLESS all the control and monitoring equipment has been tested.&nbsp; &nbsp;Ensure high MP cargoes do NOT get frozen in pipelines.&nbsp;&nbsp; A restart of cargo will be a NEW cargo operation as far as checklists are concerned.</span></i><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: #215868;
